    ELSE [u0].[username]

    ELSE [u0].[avatar_url]

    WHEN [f].[UserId1] = @__userId_0 THEN [u].[username]
    ELSE [u0].[username]
END AS [username], CASE

    ELSE [u0].[avatar_url]

To identify the code which triggers this warning, call 'ConfigureWarnings(w => w.Throw(SqlServerEventId.SavepointsDisabledBecauseOfMARS))'.
